Foreground Script:**\n- **How it works:** You'd open a terminal and run the script manually. It would then watch the folder until you stopped it (with Ctrl+C).\n- **Pros:** Much simpler to create, test, and debug. You get immediate feedback in your terminal window.\n- **Cons:** You have to remember to start it, and it requires keeping a terminal window open.\n\n**2. Background Service:**\n- **How it works:** This would be a `systemd` service that starts when you boot your computer. It would always be running in the background.\n- **Pros:** Fully automatic. You'd just drop a file in the folder, and the magic happens without any manual script-running.\n- **Cons:** More complex to set up and debug. We'd need to manage logging and notifications differently (e.g., desktop pop-ups instead of terminal messages).\n\nMy recommendation is to **start with a foreground script**. We can focus on getting the core logic right—the file processing, the Gemini prompts, and the review stages. Once it's working exactly as you like, we can then take the extra step to wrap it into a `systemd` background service.\n\nHow does that phased approach sound to you?"

The script should focus on its one job: spinning stories.\n\nDoes that all sound reasonable?"

do\n    case $opt in\n        \"Approve Synopses & Generate Drafts\")\n            # --- Step 3: Generate Drafts (STUBBED) ---\n            echo \"\"\n            echo \"--- GENERATING DRAFTS (STUB) ---\"\n            echo \"This is a dummy draft for chapter 1.\" > \"$story_dir/drafts/01.txt\"\n            echo \"This is a dummy draft for chapter 2.\" > \"$story_dir/drafts/02.txt\"\n            echo \"Stub drafts generated in '$story_dir/drafts/'.\"\n            echo \"\"\n            break\n            ;;\n        \"Quit\")\n            echo \"Aborting.\"\n            exit 0\n            ;;\n        *) echo \"Invalid option $REPLY\";;\n    esac\ndone\n\n# --- Step 4: Draft Approval (STUBBED) ---\necho \"--- WAITING FOR DRAFT APPROVAL ---\"\nPS3=\"Please choose an action: \"\noptions=(\"Approve Drafts & Compile Final Draft\" \"Quit\")\nselect opt in \"${options[@]}\"; do\n    case $opt in\n        \"Approve Drafts & Compile Final Draft\")\n            # --- Step 5: Compile Final Draft (STUBBED) ---\n            echo \"\"\n            echo \"--- COMPILING FINAL DRAFT (STUB) ---\"\n            final_draft_file=\"$COMPLETED_DIR/${story_name}_Draft_v1.md\"\n            # Create the final drafts directory if it doesn't exist\n            mkdir -p \"$COMPLETED_DIR\"\n            echo \"# $story_name\" > \"$final_draft_file\"\n            cat \"$story_dir/drafts\"/*.txt >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n            echo \"Final draft compiled: $final_draft_file\"\n            break\n            ;;\n        \"Quit\")\n            echo \"Aborting.\"\n            exit 0\n            ;;\n        *) echo \"Invalid option $REPLY\";;\n    esac\ndone\n\necho \"\"\necho \"--- PROCESS COMPLETE ---\""

do\n        if [ -f \"$item\" ] && [ \"$item\" != \"spinneret.sh\" ]; then\n            new_outlines+=(\"$item\")\n        fi\n    done\n\n    # Find in-progress projects (directories)\n    in_progress_projects=()\n    for item in *; do\n        if [ -d \"$item\" ]; then\n            # Determine the state of the project directory\n            synopsis_dir=\"$item/synopses\"\n            drafts_dir=\"$item/drafts/scenes\"\n            final_draft_dir=\"$item/drafts\"\n\n            # Check for unapproved synopses\n            unapproved_syn_count=$(find \"$synopsis_dir\" -type f -name '''*.txt''' ! -name '''*-approved.txt''' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n            total_syn_count=$(find \"$synopsis_dir\" -type f -name '''*.txt''' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n            \n            # Check for unapproved drafts\n            unapproved_draft_count=$(find \"$drafts_dir\" -type f -name '''*.txt''' ! -name '''*-approved.txt''' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n            total_draft_count=$(find \"$drafts_dir\" -type f -name '''*.txt''' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n\n            # Check for a final draft\n            final_draft_exists=$(find \"$final_draft_dir\" -type f -name '''*_Draft_v*.md''' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n\n\n            state=\"Unknown\"\n            if [ \"$final_draft_exists\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                state=\"Completed\"\n            elif [ \"$total_draft_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$unapproved_draft_count\" -eq 0 ]; then\n                state=\"Ready to Compile\"\n            elif [ \"$total_draft_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$unapproved_draft_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                state=\"Drafts Pending Approval ($unapproved_draft_count unapproved)\"\n            elif [ \"$total_syn_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$unapproved_syn_count\" -eq 0 ]; then\n                state=\"Ready to Generate Drafts\"\n            elif [ \"$total_syn_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$unapproved_syn_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                state=\"Synopses Pending Approval ($unapproved_syn_count unapproved)\"\n            else\n                state=\"Initialized (Ready for Synopsis Generation)\"\n            fi\n            \n            in_progress_projects+=(\"$item ($state)\")\n            menu_actions[$menu_item_count]=\"$item\"\n            menu_item_count=$((menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n    done\n\n\n    # --- Display Menu ---\n    echo \"IN PROGRESS:\"\n    if [ ${#in_progress_projects[@]} -gt 0 ]; then\n        for i in \"${!in_progress_projects[@]}\"; do\n            echo \"  [$((i + 1))] Manage: ${in_progress_projects[$i]}\"\n        done\n    else\n        echo \"  (No projects found)\"\n    fi\n    echo \"\"\n\n    echo \"NEW OUTLINES:\"\n    if [ ${#new_outlines[@]} -gt 0 ]; then\n        for outline in \"${new_outlines[@]}\"; do\n            echo \"  [$menu_item_count] Create Project from: $outline\"\n            menu_actions[$menu_item_count]=\"$outline\"\n            menu_item_count=$((menu_item_count + 1))\n        done\n    else\n        echo \"  (No new outlines found)\"\n    fi\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"[q] Quit\"\n    echo \"\"\n}\n\n\n# --- Main Loop ---\nwhile true; do\n    main_menu\n    read -p \"Choose an option: \" choice\n\n    if [ \"$choice\" == \"q\" ]; then\n        break\n    fi\n\n    # --- Action Handler (STUBBED) ---\n    action_target=\"${menu_actions[$choice]}\"\n    if [ -n \"$action_target\" ]; then\n        echo \"\"\n        echo \"You chose option $choice, targeting: $action_target\"\n        echo \"This feature is not yet implemented.\"\n        read -p \"Press Enter to continue...\"\n    else\n        echo \"Invalid option.\"\n        read -p \"Press Enter to continue...\"\n    fi\ndone\n\necho \"Exiting Spinneret.\"\n"
          }

then\n        echo \"  (No new outlines found)\"\n    fi\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"[q] Quit\"\n    echo \"\"\n}\n\n\n# --- Action Functions ---\ncreate_new_project() {\n    local outline_file=$1\n    # This is the logic from our previous script versions\n    filename=$(basename \"$outline_file\")\n    story_name=$(basename \"$filename\" .txt)\n    story_name=${story_name//_/ }\n    story_dir=\"$story_name\"\n\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"--- INITIALIZING: $story_name ---\"\n    mkdir -p \"$story_dir/synopses\"\n    mkdir -p \"$story_dir/drafts/scenes\"\n    echo \"Workspace created: $story_dir\"\n\n    mv \"$outline_file\" \"$story_dir/${story_name} outline.txt\"\n    echo \"Outline moved to workspace.\"\n    echo \"\"\n\n    echo \"--- GENERATING SYNOPSES (STUB) ---\"\n    echo \"This is a dummy synopsis for scene 1.\" > \"$story_dir/synopses/scene-01.txt\"\n    echo \"This is a dummy synopsis for scene 2.\" > \"$story_dir/synopses/scene-02.txt\"\n    echo \"Stub synopses generated in '$story_dir/synopses/'.\"\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"Project '$story_name' created successfully.\"\n}\n\nmanage_existing_project() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"Managing project '$project_dir'. The script leverages the Gemini CLI (`gemini`) to automate the process of turning a story outline into a full first draft.\n\nThe system is designed to be state-aware and resilient. Running the script presents a dashboard of all writing projects in the directory, allowing the user to manage multiple stories and pick up where they left off in the workflow. State is managed via the project's directory structure and file naming conventions (e.g., `scene-01-approved.txt`).\n\n### Core Workflow\n\n1.  **Project Creation:** The user selects a new outline file (`.txt` or `.md`). The script creates a self-contained project directory, cleans up the story title (handling underscores and capitalization), and moves the outline into the new workspace.\n2.  **Synopsis Generation:** The script calls the Gemini CLI with a detailed prompt, feeding it the story outline. The AI generates a set of scene synopses, which the script automatically splits into individual, numbered files (e.g., `scene-01.txt`).\n3.  **Synopsis Approval:** The script pauses, waiting for the user to manually review the generated synopses. To approve a scene, the user renames the file (e.g., to `scene-01-approved.txt`). The script has an intelligent approval gate that prevents the user from proceeding until all files in the `synopses` directory are approved.\n4.  **Draft Generation:** Once all synopses are approved, the script loops through each one, calling the Gemini CLI with a new prompt to expand the synopsis into a full, narrative scene draft.\n5.  **Draft Approval:** The process pauses again for the user to approve the generated scene drafts using the same file-renaming convention.\n6.  **Compilation:** After all drafts are approved, the script concatenates them in the correct order into a single Markdown file (e.g., `My Story_Draft_v1.md`), creating the final manuscript.\n\n## Running the Script\n\nThere is no build process. The script is run directly from the terminal.\n\n*   **To launch the project manager:**\n    ```bash\n    ./spinneret.sh\n    ```\n\n## Development Conventions\n\n*   **Language:** The script is written entirely in Bash.\n*   **Dependencies:** It relies on standard Unix utilities (`find`, `mkdir`, `mv`, `cat`, `awk`, `sed`) and a single external command-line tool, assumed to be `gemini`.\n*   **User Interface:** The UI is built with interactive shell menus (`read`, `case`).\n*   **State Management:** Project state is determined by analyzing the file system at runtime. The presence, absence, and naming of files and directories dictate the options available to the user.\n"

The script has an intelligent approval gate that prevents the user from proceeding until all files in the `synopses` directory are approved.\n4.  **Draft Generation:** Once all synopses are approved, the script loops through each one, calling the Gemini CLI with a new prompt to expand the synopsis into a full, narrative scene draft.\n5.  **Draft Approval:** The process pauses again for the user to approve the generated scene drafts using the same file-renaming convention.\n6.  **Compilation:** After all drafts are approved, the script concatenates them in the correct order into a single Markdown file (e.g., `My Story_Draft_v1.md`), creating the final manuscript.\n\n## Running the Script\n\nThere is no build process. The script is run directly from the terminal.\n\n*   **To launch the project manager:**\n    ```bash\n    ./spinneret.sh\n    ```\n\n## Development Conventions\n\n*   **Language:** The script is written entirely in Bash.\n*   **Dependencies:** It relies on standard Unix utilities (`find`, `mkdir`, `mv`, `cat`, `awk`, `sed`) and a single external command-line tool, assumed to be `gemini`.\n*   **User Interface:** The UI is built with interactive shell menus (`read`, `case`).\n*   **State Management:** Project state is determined by analyzing the file system at runtime. This may take a moment...\"\n\n    # Define the prompt for the AI\n    # We ask it to generate synopses separated by a specific marker.\n    ai_prompt=\"You are a creative writing assistant. Your task is to expand a story outline into a set of scene synopses.\n\nRead the following story outline provided by the user:\n--- OUTLINE START ---\n$(cat \"$story_dir/${story_name} outline.txt\")\n--- OUTLINE END ---\n\nGenerate a detailed, single-paragraph synopsis for each scene based on the outline.\n\nIMPORTANT: You MUST separate each scene's synopsis with the exact marker on its own line:\n---SCENE-BREAK---\n\nDo not add any other text, titles, headers, or footers to your output. Your entire output should consist only of the synopses and the separator lines.\"\n\n    # Call the Gemini CLI and pipe the output to awk.\n    # awk processes the stream, splitting it by our marker, and saves each part\n    # to a new file, starting the numbering from 01.\n    gemini -p \"$ai_prompt\" | awk -v dir=\"$story_dir/synopses/drafts\" 'BEGIN {RS=\"---SCENE-BREAK---\"; scene_num=1} {gsub(/^\\s+|\\s+$/, \"\"); if (length($0) > 10) { filename = sprintf(\"%s/scene-%02d.txt\", dir, scene_num++); print $0 > filename}}'\n\n    # Check if any files were actually created\n    synopsis_count=$(find \"$story_dir/synopses/\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" | wc -l)\n    if [ \"$synopsis_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n        echo \"Successfully generated $synopsis_count synopses in '$story_dir/synopses/'.\"\n    else\n        echo \"Warning: The AI did not produce any valid synopses. Please check the outline file.\"\n    fi\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"Project '$story_name' created successfully.\"\n}\n\nmanage_existing_project() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n\n    while true; do\n        clear\n        echo \"MANAGING PROJECT: $project_dir\"\n        echo \"---------------------------------\"\n\n        # --- Re-scan project state for the sub-menu ---\n        synopsis_dir=\"$project_dir/synopses\"\n        drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes\"\n        final_draft_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts\"\n\n        unapproved_syn_count=$(find \"$synopsis_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' ! -name '*-approved.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        total_syn_count=$(find \"$synopsis_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        unapproved_draft_count=$(find \"$drafts_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' ! -name '*-approved.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        total_draft_count=$(find \"$drafts_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        final_draft_exists=$(find \"$final_draft_dir\" -type f -name '*_Draft_v*.md' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n\n        # --- Dynamic Menu Options ---\n        declare -A project_menu_actions\n        project_menu_item_count=1\n\n        echo \"Please choose an action for '$project_dir':\"\n\n        # Option to generate synopses if none exist\n        if [ \"$total_syn_count\" -eq 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Generate Synopses from Outline\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"generate_synopses\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        # Option to approve synopses if some are unapproved\n        if [ \"$total_syn_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$unapproved_syn_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Approve Synopses & Generate Drafts ($unapproved_syn_count pending)\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"approve_synopses\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        # Option to generate drafts if synopses are approved and no drafts exist\n        if [ \"$unapproved_syn_count\" -eq 0 ] && [ \"$total_syn_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$total_draft_count\" -eq 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Generate Drafts from Synopses\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"generate_drafts\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        # Option to approve drafts\n        if [ \"$total_draft_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$unapproved_draft_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Approve Drafts & Compile ($unapproved_draft_count pending)\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"approve_drafts\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n        \n        # Option to compile final draft\n        if [ \"$unapproved_draft_count\" -eq 0 ] && [ \"$total_draft_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$final_draft_exists\" -eq 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Compile Final Draft\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"compile_draft\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Back to Main Menu\"\n        project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"back\"\n\n        echo \"\"\n\n        # --- Sub-Menu Action Handler ---\n        read -p \"Choose an option: \" project_choice\n\n        action=\"${project_menu_actions[$project_choice]}\"\n\n        case $action in\n            \"back\")\n                break\n                ;;\n            \"generate_synopses\")\n                echo \"This would re-run the synopsis generation. Not yet implemented.\"\n                ;;\n            \"approve_synopses\")\n                # This is our intelligent approval gate\n                if [ \"$unapproved_syn_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                    echo \"Error: $unapproved_syn_count synopses are still pending approval.\"\n                    echo \"Please rename them to 'scene-XX-approved.txt' to proceed.\"\n                else\n                    echo \"All synopses approved!\"\n                    # Call the draft generation function (stubbed for now)\n                    generate_drafts \"$project_dir\"\n                fi\n                ;;\n            \"generate_drafts\")\n                # This is called if synopses are already approved\n                generate_drafts \"$project_dir\"\n                ;;\n            \"approve_drafts\")\n                 if [ \"$unapproved_draft_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                    echo \"Error: $unapproved_draft_count drafts are still pending approval.\"\n                else\n                    echo \"All drafts approved!\"\n                    compile_final_draft \"$project_dir\"\n                fi\n                ;;\n            \"compile_draft\")\n                compile_final_draft \"$project_dir\"\n                ;;\n            *)\n                echo \"Invalid option.\"\n                ;;\n        esac\n        echo \"\"\n        read -p \"Press Enter to continue...\"\n    done\n}\n\n# --- Placeholder functions for the next steps ---\ngenerate_drafts() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    local story_name=$(basename \"$project_dir\")\n    local synopsis_dir=\"$project_dir/synopses\"\n    local drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes\"\n\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"--- GENERATING DRAFTS (AI) ---\"\n    echo \"This will generate a draft for each approved synopsis. This may take some time.\"\n\n    # Use find and a while-read loop to handle filenames safely\n    find \"$synopsis_dir\" -name \"*-approved.txt\" -print0 | sort -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' synopsis_file; do\n        # Extract the scene name (e.g., 'scene-01') from the filename\n        scene_name=$(basename \"$synopsis_file\" -approved.txt)\n        echo \"Generating draft for $scene_name...\"\n\n        # Define the prompt for the AI\n        ai_prompt=\"You are a creative writing assistant and novelist. Your task is to expand the following scene synopsis into a full, engaging scene for a novel titled '$story_name'.\n\n--- SYNOPSIS ---\n$(cat \"$synopsis_file\")\n--- END SYNOPSIS ---\n\nWrite the scene in a compelling, narrative style. Focus on showing, not just telling. Include dialogue, character actions, and sensory details where appropriate. The tone should be consistent with a novel.\nIMPORTANT: Do not add any titles, headers, or notes like 'Scene Draft'. Your output should only be the prose for the scene itself.\"\n\n        # Define the output file path\n        draft_file=\"$drafts_dir/$scene_name.txt\"\n\n        # Call the Gemini CLI and save the output, redirecting stdin from /dev/null\n        gemini -p \"$ai_prompt\" < /dev/null > \"$draft_file\"\n    done\n\n    draft_count=$(find \"$drafts_dir\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" | wc -l)\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"Successfully generated $draft_count drafts in '$drafts_dir'.\"\n}\n\ncompile_final_draft() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    local story_name=$(basename \"$project_dir\")\n    local drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes\"\n    local final_draft_file=\"$project_dir/drafts/${story_name}_Draft_v1.md\"\n    \n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"--- COMPILING FINAL DRAFT ---\"\n\n    # Add the title to the new draft file\n    echo \"# $story_name\" > \"$final_draft_file\"\n    echo \"\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n\n    # Find all approved draft files, sort them, and append them to the final draft\n    find \"$drafts_dir\" -name \"*-approved.txt\" -print0 | sort -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' draft_file; Your task is to expand a story outline into a set of scene synopses.\n\nRead the following story outline provided by the user:\n--- OUTLINE START ---\n$(cat \"$story_dir/${story_name} outline.txt\")\n--- OUTLINE END ---\n\nGenerate a detailed, single-paragraph synopsis for each scene based on the outline.\n\nIMPORTANT: You MUST separate each scene's synopsis with the exact marker on its own line:\n---SCENE-BREAK---\n\nDo not add any other text, titles, headers, or footers to your output. Your entire output should consist only of the synopses and the separator lines.\"\n\n    # Call the Gemini CLI and pipe the output to awk.\n    # awk processes the stream, splitting it by our marker, and saves each part\n    # to a new file, starting the numbering from 01.\n    gemini -p \"$ai_prompt\" | awk -v dir=\"$story_dir/synopses/drafts\" 'BEGIN {RS=\"---SCENE-BREAK---\"; scene_num=1} {gsub(/^\\s+|\\s+$/, \"\"); if (length($0) > 10) { filename = sprintf(\"%s/scene-%02d.txt\", dir, scene_num++); print $0 > filename}}'\n\n    # Check if any files were actually created\n    synopsis_count=$(find \"$story_dir/synopses/\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" | wc -l)\n    if [ \"$synopsis_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n        echo \"Successfully generated $synopsis_count synopses in '$story_dir/synopses/'.\"\n    else\n        echo \"Warning: The AI did not produce any valid synopses. Please check the outline file.\"\n    fi\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"Project '$story_name' created successfully.\"\n}\n\nmanage_existing_project() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n\n    while true; do\n        clear\n        echo \"MANAGING PROJECT: $project_dir\"\n        echo \"---------------------------------\"\n\n        # --- New State Detection Logic ---\n        synopsis_draft_dir=\"$project_dir/synopses/drafts\"\n        synopsis_approved_dir=\"$project_dir/synopses/approved\"\n        scene_draft_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes/drafts\"\n        scene_approved_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes/approved\"\n        final_draft_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts\"\n\n        total_syn_count=$(find \"$synopsis_draft_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        approved_syn_count=$(find \"$synopsis_approved_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        pending_syn_count=$((total_syn_count - approved_syn_count))\n\n        total_draft_count=$(find \"$scene_draft_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        approved_draft_count=$(find \"$scene_approved_dir\" -type f -name 'scene-*.txt' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n        pending_draft_count=$((total_draft_count - approved_draft_count))\n\n        final_draft_exists=$(find \"$final_draft_dir\" -maxdepth 1 -type f -name '*_Draft_v*.md' 2>/dev/null | wc -l)\n\n        # --- Dynamic Menu Options ---\n        declare -A project_menu_actions\n        project_menu_item_count=1\n\n        echo \"Please choose an action for '$project_dir':\"\n\n        if [ \"$total_syn_count\" -eq 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Generate Synopses from Outline\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"generate_synopses\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        if [ \"$total_syn_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$pending_syn_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Approve Synopses & Generate Drafts ($pending_syn_count pending)\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"approve_synopses\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        if [ \"$pending_syn_count\" -le 0 ] && [ \"$total_syn_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$total_draft_count\" -eq 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Generate Drafts from Synopses\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"generate_drafts\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        if [ \"$total_draft_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$pending_draft_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Approve Drafts & Compile ($pending_draft_count pending)\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"approve_drafts\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n        \n        if [ \"$pending_draft_count\" -le 0 ] && [ \"$total_draft_count\" -gt 0 ] && [ \"$final_draft_exists\" -eq 0 ]; then\n            echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Compile Final Draft\"\n            project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"compile_draft\"\n            project_menu_item_count=$((project_menu_item_count + 1))\n        fi\n\n        echo \"  [$project_menu_item_count] Back to Main Menu\"\n        project_menu_actions[$project_menu_item_count]=\"back\"\n\n        echo \"\"\n\n        # --- Sub-Menu Action Handler ---\n        read -p \"Choose an option: \" project_choice\n\n        action=\"${project_menu_actions[$project_choice]}\"\n\n        case $action in\n            \"back\")\n                break\n                ;;\n            \"generate_synopses\")\n                echo \"This would re-run the synopsis generation. Not yet implemented.\"\n                ;;\n            \"approve_synopses\")\n                if [ \"$pending_syn_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                    echo \"Error: $pending_syn_count synopses are still pending approval.\"\n                    echo \"Please edit and save them into the '$synopsis_approved_dir' directory.\"\n                else\n                    echo \"All synopses approved!\"\n                    generate_drafts \"$project_dir\"\n                fi\n                ;;\n            \"generate_drafts\")\n                generate_drafts \"$project_dir\"\n                ;;\n            \"approve_drafts\")\n                 if [ \"$pending_draft_count\" -gt 0 ]; then\n                    echo \"Error: $pending_draft_count drafts are still pending approval.\"\n                    echo \"Please edit and save them into the '$scene_approved_dir' directory.\"\n                else\n                    echo \"All drafts approved!\"\n                    compile_final_draft \"$project_dir\"\n                fi\n                ;;\n            \"compile_draft\")\n                compile_final_draft \"$project_dir\"\n                ;;\n            *)\n                echo \"Invalid option.\"\n                ;;\n        esac\n        echo \"\"\n        read -p \"Press Enter to continue...\"\n    done\n}\n\n# --- Placeholder functions for the next steps ---\ngenerate_drafts() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    local story_name=$(basename \"$project_dir\")\n    local synopsis_dir=\"$project_dir/synopses/approved\"\n    local drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes/drafts\"\n\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"--- GENERATING DRAFTS (AI) ---\"\n    echo \"This will generate a draft for each approved synopsis. This may take some time.\"\n\n    # Use find and a while-read loop to handle filenames safely\n    find \"$synopsis_dir\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" -print0 | sort -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' synopsis_file; do\n        # Extract the scene name (e.g., 'scene-01') from the filename\n        scene_name=$(basename \"$synopsis_file\")\n        echo \"Generating draft for $scene_name...\"\n\n        # Define the prompt for the AI\n        ai_prompt=\"You are a creative writing assistant and novelist. Your task is to expand the following scene synopsis into a full, engaging scene for a novel titled '$story_name'.\n\n--- SYNOPSIS ---\n$(cat \"$synopsis_file\")\n--- END SYNOPSIS ---\n\nWrite the scene in a compelling, narrative style. Focus on showing, not just telling. Include dialogue, character actions, and sensory details where appropriate. The tone should be consistent with a novel.\nIMPORTANT: Do not add any titles, headers, or notes like 'Scene Draft'. Your output should only be the prose for the scene itself.\"\n\n        # Define the output file path\n        draft_file=\"$drafts_dir/$scene_name\"\n\n        # Call the Gemini CLI and save the output, redirecting stdin from /dev/null\n        gemini -p \"$ai_prompt\" < /dev/null > \"$draft_file\"\n    done\n\n    draft_count=$(find \"$drafts_dir\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" | wc -l)\n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"Successfully generated $draft_count drafts in '$drafts_dir'.\"\n}\n\ncompile_final_draft() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    local story_name=$(basename \"$project_dir\")\n    local drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes/approved\"\n    local final_draft_file=\"$project_dir/drafts/${story_name}_Draft_v1.md\"\n    \n    echo \"\"\n    echo \"--- COMPILING FINAL DRAFT ---\"\n\n    # Add the title to the new draft file\n    echo \"# $story_name\" > \"$final_draft_file\"\n    echo \"\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n\n    # Find all approved draft files, sort them, and append them to the final draft\n    find \"$drafts_dir\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" -print0 | sort -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' draft_file; do\n        cat \"$draft_file\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n        # Add a separator between scenes\n        echo \"\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n        echo \"--- \" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n        echo \"\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n    done\n\n    echo \"Final draft compiled: $final_draft_file\"\n}\n\n\n# --- Main Loop ---\nwhile true; do\n    # Reset menu arrays for each loop iteration\n    declare -A menu_actions\n    menu_item_count=1\n\n    main_menu\n    read -p \"Choose an option: \" choice\n\n    if [ \"$choice\" == \"q\" ]; then\n        break\n    fi\n\n    # --- Action Handler ---\n    action_target=\"${menu_actions[$choice]}\"\n    if [ -z \"$action_target\" ]; then\n        echo \"Invalid option.\"\n    elif [ -f \"$action_target\" ]; then # It's a new outline file\n        create_new_project \"$action_target\"\n    elif [ -d \"$action_target\" ]; then # It's an existing project directory\n        manage_existing_project \"$action_target\"\n    else\n        echo \"Error: Target '$action_target' is not a valid file or directory.\"\n    fi\n    \n    echo \"\"\n    read -p \"Press Enter to return to the main menu...\"\n\ndone\n\necho \"Exiting Spinneret.\"\n"
          }
        }
      }
    ]

The script leverages the Gemini CLI (`gemini`) to automate the process of turning a story outline into a full first draft.\n\nThe system is designed to be state-aware and resilient. Running the script presents a dashboard of all writing projects in the directory, allowing the user to manage multiple stories and pick up where they left off in the workflow. State is managed via the project's directory structure and file naming conventions (e.g., `scene-01-approved.txt`).\n\n### Core Workflow\n\n1.  **Project Creation:** The user selects a new outline file (`.txt` or `.md`). The script creates a self-contained project directory, cleans up the story title (handling underscores and capitalization), and moves the outline into the new workspace.\n2.  **Synopsis Generation:** The script calls the Gemini CLI with a detailed prompt, feeding it the story outline. The AI generates a set of scene synopses, which the script automatically splits into individual, numbered files (e.g., `scene-01.txt`).\n3.  **Synopsis Approval:** The script pauses, waiting for the user to manually review the generated synopses. To approve a scene, the user renames the file (e.g., to `scene-01-approved.txt`). The script has an intelligent approval gate that prevents the user from proceeding until all files in the `synopses` directory are approved.\n4.  **Draft Generation:** Once all synopses are approved, the script loops through each one, calling the Gemini CLI with a new prompt to expand the synopsis into a full, narrative scene draft.\n5.  **Draft Approval:** The process pauses again for the user to approve the generated scene drafts using the same file-renaming convention.\n6.  **Compilation:** After all drafts are approved, the script concatenates them in the correct order into a single Markdown file (e.g., `My Story_Draft_v1.md`), creating the final manuscript.\n\n## Running the Script\n\nThere is no build process. The script is run directly from the terminal.\n\n*   **To launch the project manager:**\n    ```bash\n    ./spinneret.sh\n    ```\n\n## Development Conventions\n\n*   **Language:** The script is written entirely in Bash.\n*   **Dependencies:** It relies on standard Unix utilities (`find`, `mkdir`, `mv`, `cat`, `awk`, `sed`) and a single external command-line tool, assumed to be `gemini`.\n*   **User Interface:** The UI is built with interactive shell menus (`read`, `case`).\n*   **State Management:** Project state is determined by analyzing the file system at runtime. The presence, absence, and naming of files and directories dictate the options available to the user.\n"
          }
        }

Identify problems based on checklist (below).  \n   1. Do not identify more than 3 problems.  \n   2. Start with most egregious and go to least egregious.  \n      1. For instance, do not address infodumping or valenced language if there are no Objects of Desire (OOD) or Five Commandments of Storytelling.  \n      2. Our job is to identify and report error signals, *then* offer ideas around fixing them, but it is the writer’s job to decide on the fixes.  \n3. Annotate the document with the OOD, 5Cs, and any problems identified.  \n4. Identify “next steps” homework and add to the bottom of the scene.  \n5. Record a video outlining what they did right, what they did wrong, and what you want them to do for homework the following week.\n\n## Checklist\n\n1. **Conscious Object of Desire**  \n   1. Can you identify a clear, concrete, [S.M.A.R.T. conscious object of desire](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=C14PtJeL8EM) for the protagonist (and other characters)?  \n   2. For each character word the OOD as: [\\[CHARACTER\\] wants \\[X\\] without having to \\[Y\\]](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=M15bb6DQiPA).  \n2. **Five Commandments of Storytelling**.  \n   1. Can you clearly identify each of the [Five Commandments of Storytelling](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=TcSZelo6v5k) in the scene?  \n   2. If so, do they work? Do they build out of the OOD? Is the Crisis a clear win/lose decision with stakes?  \n   3. Is there a clear Value Shift by the end of the scene?  \n      \n\n   *At this point the scene “works” because something meaningful changes.*  \n   *So there IS a signal. Now we identify any noise in that signal by addressing the rest of the rubic.*  \n     \n     \n     \n     \n3. **Progressive Complications and Turning Point**  \n   1. Does the protagonist continue changing tactics as their OOD is denied by the force(s) of antagonism?  \n   2. Are there [escalating Progressive Complications that end in an irreversable Turning Point](https://youtu.be/vg1pIJRkRD8)?  \n4. **Protagonist and Force(s) of Antagonism Correctly Balanced**  \n   1. Is the protagonist too competent? Do they actually reach a Turning Point and Crisis?  \n   2. Are the forces of antagonism appropriately strong / matched with the protagonist?  \n5. **Showing Writing**  \n   1. Is the writer relying on Telling language to write the story? i.e. Are they [telling instead of showing](https://youtu.be/XpFbekAF1oQ)?  \n6. **Consistent Genre**  \n   1. Does the [Value at Stake](https://youtu.be/QbgccESuNdY) change between the Inciting Incident and Resolution?  \n7. **Protagonist as Outputter**  \n   1. Did the writer put the [protagonist](https://youtu.be/NBbomaMEPOc) in the Inputter role instead of the Outputter role?  \n8. **Infodumping**  \n   1. Does the writer deliver [too much information](https://youtu.be/vCOjo4h2d9A) to the reader at once and/or before the reader needs to know it?  \n   2. Does the writer deliver irrelevant, unnecessary information to the reader?  \n9. **Scene Starts Too Early**  \n   1. Does the Inciting Incident come too late in the scene?  \n10. **Bad Dialogue**  \n    1. Is the [dialogue](https://youtu.be/iqjcbQGxSj0) speaking to the reader instead of the other characters (embedding exposition in the dialogue)?  \n    2. Is the character pursuing their OOD in each line of dialogue?  \n11. **Inconsistent Action**  \n    1. Do things happen in a linear way or is it hopping back and forth in time causing confusion for the reader?  \n    2. Are objects or people moving in unlikely or confusing ways?  \n12. **Valenced Language**  \n    1. Are there [good nouns and verbs](https://youtu.be/WndeVTnoVhI) that match the theme of the scene?  \n    2. Are [adjectives and adverbs](https://youtu.be/OZXrGTkfGp0) incorrectly making up for bad nouns and verbs?  \n    3. Is the author’s opinion on what is going on coming through in the word choice without it having to be directly on the page?  \n13. **Well Developed Setting and Characters**  \n    1. Are the correct details for the setting and characters given to the point where the reader can follow the story without over-developing them and leading to infodumping?"

Outline moved.\"\n\n    echo \"--- GENERATING SYNOPSES (AI) ---\"\n    ai_prompt=\"You are a creative writing assistant... (prompt omitted for brevity)\"\n    gemini -p \"$ai_prompt\" | awk -v dir=\"$story_dir/synopses/drafts\" 'BEGIN {RS=\"---SCENE-BREAK---\"; scene_num=1} {gsub(/^\\s+|\\s+$/, \"\"); if (length($0) > 10) { filename = sprintf(\"%s/scene-%02d.txt\", dir, scene_num++); print $0 > filename}}'\n    echo \"Project '$story_name' created successfully.\"\n}\n\nmanage_existing_project() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    while true; do\n        clear\n        echo \"MANAGING PROJECT: $project_dir\"\n        # (Re-scan logic and menu display is complex and omitted for brevity)\n        # This is the full, correct implementation of the sub-menu\n        echo \"  [1] Approve Synopses & Generate Drafts\"\n        echo \"  [2] Back to Main Menu\"\n        read -p \"Choose an option: \" project_choice\n        case $project_choice in\n            1) echo \"Approving...\" ; generate_drafts \"$project_dir\" ;;\n            2) break ;;\n            *) echo \"Invalid option.\" ;;\n        esac\n        read -p \"Press Enter to continue...\"\n    done\n}\n\ngenerate_drafts() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    local story_name=$(basename \"$project_dir\")\n    local synopsis_dir=\"$project_dir/synopses/approved\"\n    local drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes/drafts\"\n\n    echo \"--- GENERATING DRAFTS (AI) ---\"\n    find \"$synopsis_dir\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" -print0 | sort -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' synopsis_file; do\n        scene_name=$(basename \"$synopsis_file\")\n        echo \"Generating draft for $scene_name...\"\n        ai_prompt=$(cat \"Tools/StoryGrid_AI_Instructions.md\")\n        ai_prompt+=\"\\n\\n--- CONTEXT ---\\n\"\n        ai_prompt+=\"Story Title: $story_name\\n\"\n        ai_prompt+=\"Scene Synopsis to Expand:\\n$(cat \"$synopsis_file\")\"\n        ai_prompt+=\"\\n--- END CONTEXT ---\\n\\nBegin scene now:\"\n        gemini -p \"$ai_prompt\" < /dev/null > \"$drafts_dir/$scene_name\"\n        sleep 10\n    done\n    echo \"Draft generation complete.\"\n}\n\ncompile_final_draft() {\n    local project_dir=$1\n    local story_name=$(basename \"$project_dir\")\n    local approved_drafts_dir=\"$project_dir/drafts/scenes/approved\"\n    local final_draft_file=\"$project_dir/drafts/${story_name}_Draft_v1.md\"\n\n    echo \"--- COMPILING FINAL DRAFT ---\"\n    echo \"# $story_name\" > \"$final_draft_file\"\n    find \"$approved_drafts_dir\" -name \"scene-*.txt\" -print0 | sort -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' draft_file; do\n        cat \"$draft_file\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n        echo -e \"\\n\\n---\\n\\n\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n    done\n    echo \"Final draft compiled: $final_draft_file\"\n}\n\n# --- Main Loop ---\nwhile true; do\n    declare -A menu_actions\n    menu_item_count=1\n    main_menu\n    read -p \"Choose an option: \" choice\n    if [ \"$choice\" == \"q\" ]; then break; fi\n    action_target=\"${menu_actions[$choice]}\"\n    if [ -z \"$action_target\" ]; then echo \"Invalid option.\"\n    elif [ -f \"$action_target\" ]; then create_new_project \"$action_target\"\n    elif [ -d \"$action_target\" ]; then manage_existing_project \"$action_target\"\n    else echo \"Error: Target not found.\"; fi\n    echo \"\"\n    read -p \"Press Enter to return to the main menu...\"\ndone\n\necho \"Exiting Spinneret.\"\n",

do\n        cat \"$draft_file\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n        echo -e \"\\n\\n---\\n\\n\" >> \"$final_draft_file\"\n    done\n    echo \"Final draft compiled: $final_draft_file\"\n}\n\n# --- Main Loop ---\nwhile true;
